9a6('bum): dag par spong ba rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ yang dag par spong ba nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang yang dag par spong ba rnamaso//

9a8('bum): so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnam so// dbang po rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ dbang po rna las las gud na yang chos kyi dbyangs ma mchis te/ dbang po rnams
9b1('bum): kyang chos kyi dbying so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dbang po rnam so// stobs rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ stobs rnams las gung na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ 
9b2('bum): stobs nyid kyang chos kyi dbying sa// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang stobs rnamaso// byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags byang chub kyi yan lag rnams las gung
9b3('bum): na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ byang chub kyi yan lag nyid kyang chos kyi dbying sa// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang byang chub kyi yan lag rnam so// lam yang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lam
9b4('bum): las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lam/ nyid kyang chos kyi dbyingaso// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lam mo// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams kyang chos
9b5('bum): kyi dbyings ma lags/ 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyingaso// chos kyi
9b6('bum): dbyings nyid kyang 'phag dri bden gam so// bsam gtan rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ bsam gtan rnam las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ bsam gtan nyid kyang chos kyi
9b7('bum): dbyeng so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang bsam gtan rnam so// tshad med pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ tshad med pa rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ tshad
9b8('bum): med pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyingaso// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang tshad med pa rnam so// gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags// gzugs med pa'i snyom par 'jug pa
10a1('bum): rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzugs med
10a2('bum): pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams so// rnam par thar pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rnam par thar pa rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rnam par thar pa
10a3('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par thar pa rnams so// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mthar gyis gnas

10a5('bum): nyid kyang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rna mas so// rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa yang chos kyi dbyings ma lags
10a6('bum): rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med
10a7('bum): pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'o// mngon par shes pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ 
10a8('bum): mngon par shes pa rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ mngon par shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mngon par shes pa rnams so// ting nge 'dzin
10b1('bum): rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ ting nge 'dzin rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ ting nge 'dzin nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang ting nge 'dzin
10b2('bum): rnams so// gzungs kyi sgo rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ gzungs kyi sgo nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos
10b3('bum): kyi dbyings nyid kyang gzung skye sgo rnams so// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings
10b4('bum): ma mchis te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams gyi mi 'jigs pa rnams kyang
10b5('bum): chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ mi 'jigs pa rnams la sa gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ mi 'jigs/ pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyingaso// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang mi 'jig
10b6('bum): pa rnams so// so so yang dag par rig pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ so so yang dag par rig pa rnams las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ so so yang dag par rig pa
10b7('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang so so yang dag par rig pa rnam so// byams pa chen po yang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ byams pa chen po las gud na chos kyi dbyings ma mchis
10b8('bum): te/ byams pa chen po nyid kyang chos kyi dbying so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang byams chen po'o// snying rje chen po yang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ snying rje chen po las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ 
11a1('bum): snying rje chen po nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang snying rje chen po'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ sangs rgyas

11a3('bum): so// rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu yang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings so// /

11b1('bum): byang chub bo// lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings ma lags/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid las gud na yang chos kyi dbyings ma mchis te/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid kyang chos

15a2('bum): nyid kyang snying rje chen po'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbying so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnam so// rgyun tu zhugs pa'i

15a4('bum): cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu nyid kyang chos kyi dbyingaso// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// dgra bco
15a5('bum): ba nyid kyang chos dbying so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang dgra bcom/ pa'o// rang byang chub nyid kyang chos kyi dbyings// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rang byang chub po// lam gyi rnam pa shes pa
15a6('bum): nyid kyang chos kyi dbying so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid do// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyang chos kyi dbying so// chos kyi dbyings nyid kyang rnam pa thams cad
15a7('bum): mkhyen pa nyid do// rab 'byor gal te yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe// chos kyi dbyings la ma gtogs pa'i chos 'gra' zhig mthog
15a8('bum): nanini bla na med pa yang dag por rdzogs pa'i byang chub la gnas par yang mi 'gyur te/ chos thams cad ni chos kyi dbyings yin pas/ de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi
15b1('bum): rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ chos thams cad chos kyi dbyings su shes nas/ chos thams cad ming med pa lnga ming gi brdas chos ston te/ 'di ni gzugs shes bya'o// 'di ni tsher ba zhe/ 
15b2('bum): bya'o 'di ni 'du shes zhes bya'o// 'di ni 'du byed ces bya'o// 'di ni rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni mig ces bya'o// 'di ni rna ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni sna zhes bya'o// 'di ni
15b3('bum): zhes bya'o/ 'di ni lus zhes bya'o// 'di ni yod ces bya'o// 'di ni gzugs shes bya'o// 'di ni sgra zhes bya'o// 'di ni dr-i zhes bya'o// 'di ni ro zhes bya'o// 'di ni reg ces bya'o// 'di ni chos
15b4('bum): zhes bya'o// 'di ni mig gi rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// / 'di ni rna ba'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni sna'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni lce'i rnam par shes
15b5('bum): zhes bya'o// 'di ni lus kyi rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni riH/ gi 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa
15b6('bum): zhes bya'o/ 'di ni sna'i 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni lce'i 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di/ ni lus kyi 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni yid kyi 'dus te reg pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni
15b7('bum): mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'dri ni sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni 'i
15b8('bum): 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'o ni lus kyi 'dus te rig pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni yid kyi lasu te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni sa'i
16a1('bum): zhes bya'o// 'di ni chu'i khams zhes bya'o// 'di ni me'i khams zhes bya'o// 'di ni rlung gi khams shes bya'o// 'di ni nam mkha'i khams zhes bya'o// 'di ni rnam par shes pa'i kha
16a2('bum): zhes bya'o/ 'di ni ma rig pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni 'du byed ces bya'o// 'di ni rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni ming dang gzugs zhes bya'o// 'di ni skye mched drug ces bya'o// 'di ni reg pa zhes bya'o// 
16a3('bum): 'di ni tshor ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni sred pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni len pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni srid pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni skye ba zhes bya'o// 'di ni rga shi zhes bya'o// 'di ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni
16a4('bum): tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni brtson 'grus kyi pha/ rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni bsam gtan gyis pha rol
16a5('bum): tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// 'di ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa/ zhes bya'o// 'di ni nang stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni phyi stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni phyi nang stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 
16a6('bum): 'di ni stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni chen po stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni don dam pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni 'dus byas stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ces
16a7('bum): bya'o// 'di ni mtha' las 'das po stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni thog ma dang sha ma med pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni rang bzhin stong pa nyid ces bya'o/ 
16a8('bum): 'di ni chos thams cad stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 
16b1('bum): 'di ni ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di dag ni dran pa nye bar bzhag pa rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni yang dgu par spong ba rnams
16b2('bum): shes bya'o// 'di dag ni rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni dbang po rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni stobs rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni byang chub kyi yan lag rnams
16b3('bum): shes bya'o// 'di dag ni 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni bsam gtan rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni
16b4('bum): tshad med pa rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni gzugs med/ pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni rnam par thar pa brgyad ces bya'o// 'di dag ni mthar gyis
16b5('bum): gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu zhes bya'o// 'di na ni rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni mngon par shes
16b6('bum): pa rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni ting nge 'dzin rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni gzungs kyi sgo rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni mi
16b7('bum): 'jigs pa rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni so so yang dag par rig pa rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni byams pa chen po zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni snying rje chen po zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni sa sam kyi chos
16b8('bum): ma 'dres pa rnams shes bya'o// 'di dag ni rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu zhes bya'o// 'di dag ni lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu zhes bya'o// 'di ni phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu zhes bya'o// 'di ni dgra
17a1('bum): bcom pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni rang byang chub ces bya'o// 'di ni lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid ces bya'o// 'di ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ces bya'o zhes chos na
17a2('bum): to// rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/ sgyu ma'i mkhan po 'am/ sgyu ma byed pa'i mtshan du mkhas pa zhig gis rdzas kyi rnam pagyin zhig la brten nas/ gzugs kyi bye brag sna tshogs 'di lta ste
17a3('bum): glang po'i gzugs sam/ rta'i gzugs sam// baglang gi gzugs sam// rnga mo dang lug gi gzugs sam/ skyes pa dang bud med dang / khye'u dang bu mo'i gzugs sam/ skyed mos tshal
17a4('bum): dang gzhal med khang dang / dka' thub kyi nags tshal da dang / kun dga'i rab mdangs dga' ba 'am/ rdzing bu dmadangs dga' ba 'am/ nags 'tshal mdangs dga' ba
17a5('bum): dgra sprul cing de dag tu stan dang / 'khor gyi stan dang / gzhi rnam pa sna tshogs bting ste/ me tog dang / phreng ba dang / spos dang / byug pa dang / kha zas dang / spyan
17a6('bum): gzigs zhim po dag bstan tam/ glu dang sil snyan gyis skye bo dga' bar byas sam/ sbyin pa yongs su btang ba 'am/ tshul khrims bsrung ba 'am/ bzod pa bsgrub po 'am/ 
17a7('bum): brtson 'grus brtsam pa 'am/ ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam par brtse ba 'am/ shes rab bsgom pa 'am/ rnam pa de lta bu dag gis skye bo dga' bar byas te/ rgyal rigs che zhing mtho ba'i
17a8('bum): rigs bstan tam/ bram ze che zhing mtho ba'i rigs bstan tam/ khyim bdag che zhing mtho ba'i rigs bstan tam/ ri rab bstan tam/ rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams bstan tam/ sum bcu rtsa/ 
17b1('bum): gsum gyi lha rnams bstan tam/ mtsho ma'i lha rnams bstan tam/ dga' ldan gyi lha rnams bstan tam/ 'phrul dga'i lha rnams bstan tam/ gzhin 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams
17b2('bum): tam tshangs ris kyi lha rnams bstan tam/ tshangs lha nye phan gyi lha rnams bstan tam/ tshangs pa kun 'khor gyi lha rnams bstan tan/ tshangs chen gyi lha rnams bstan tam/ snang ba'i lha
17b3('bum): rnams bstan tam// chung snang gi lha rnams bstan tam/ tshad med snang ba'i lha rnams bstan tam/ kun snang dang ba'i lha rnams bstan tam/ dge ba'i lha rnams bstan tam// chung dge'i lha rnams
17b4('bum): bstan tam/ tshad med dge ba'i lha rnams bstan tam// dge rgyas kyi lha rnams bstan tam// che ba'i lha rnam/ bstan tam/ chung che'i lha rnams bstan tam/ tshang
17b5('bum): med che ba'i lha rnams bstan tam/ 'bras bu che ba'i lte rnams bstan tam/ mi che ba'i lha rnams bstan tam/ mi gdung ba'i lha rnams bstan tam/ shin tu mthong ba'i lha
17b6('bum): rnams bstan tam/ gya nom snang ba'i lha rnams bstun tam/ 'og min gyi lha rnams bstan tam// nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched kyi lha rnams bstan tam/ rnam shes mtha' yas skye
17b7('bum): mched kyi lha rnams bstan tam/ chung zad mang ba'i skye mched kyi lha rnams bstan tam/ 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi lha gzugs med pa rnams bstan tam/ rgyun tu zhugs pa/ 
17b8('bum): dang lan cig phyir 'ong ba 'am/ phyir mi 'ong ba dang / dgra bcom pa dang / rang sangs rgyas mang po bstan tam/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sems dang po bskyed pa nas/ nye bar brdung / 
18a1('bum): steng sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi pha rol
18a2('bum): tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / nang stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / phyi stong pa nyid la spyod
18a3('bum): pa dang phyi nang stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / chen po stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / don dam pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / 'dus byas stong pa nyid
18a4('bum): la spyod pa dang / 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la spyod pa / mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / ngor
18a5('bum): ba med pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / rang bzhin stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / chos thams cad stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la spyod pa
18a6('bum): dang / mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / 
18a7('bum): dran pa nye bar bzhag pa rnams la spyod pa dang / yang dag par spong ba rnams la spyod pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la spyod pa dang / dbang po rnams la spyod pa dang / stobs rnams
18a8('bum): la spyod pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la spyod pa dang / 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la spyod pa dang / bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par
18b1('bum): 'dug pa la spong ba dang / sa dang po yongasu rdzogs par byed ba dang / sa gnyis su rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa gsum pa yongasu rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa bzhi pa yong su rdzogs par byed pa dang // 
18b2('bum): sa lnga pa yong su rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa drug pa yongasu rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa bdun pa yongasu rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa brdung ba yongasu rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa dgu pa yongasu
18b3('bum): rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa bcu pa yong su rdzogs par byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa la 'dug pa dang / mngon par shes pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / mngon par shes pa
18b4('bum): de dag gis rnam par rtse zhing 'jig rten gyi khams snang bar dbyed pa dang / sems can rnams yongasu smin par/ byed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongasu dag par byed pa dang
18b5('bum): yan lag dang nying lag thams cad yongasu gtong ba dang / spyad par dka' ba'i spyad pa spyod pa dang / de bzhin gshe gos pa'i stobs rnams yongasu sgrub pa dang / mi 'jigs
18b6('bum): pa rnams yongasu sgrub pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa rnams yongasu sgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams yongasu sgrub pa dang / snying rje chen po mngon par bsgrub pa de
18b7('bum): dag bstan tam/ sangs rgyas kyi sku yan lag dang nying lag yongasu rdzogs pa bstan na/ de la sems can khyis pa'i ngang tshul can 'di snyam du sems te/ kye ma mi 'dis legs par
18b8('bum): bslabs pa ngo mtshar che'o re mdzes dag byed/ de ltar skye bo dga' bar byed cing / gzugs kyi bye brag sna tshogs 'di lta ste/ glang po'i gzugs dang / rta'i gzugs dang / ba glang gi
19a1('bum): gzugs dang / rnga mo dang lug gi gzugs dang / skyes pa dang / bud med dang / khye'u dang ga bu mo'i gzugs ston pa dang / skyed mos tshal dang / gzhal med khang dang / 
19a2('bum): dka' thub kyi nags tshal dang / kun dga'i ra ba mdangs dga' ba ston pa dang / rdzing bu mdangs dga' ba ston pa dang / nags tshal mdangs dga' ba ston pa dang / de dag tu stan dang
19a3('bum): 'khor gyi stan dang / gzhi rnam pa sna tshogs bting ste/ me tog dang / phreng ba dang / spos dang / byug pa dang / phye ma dang / kha zas dang / spyan gzigs mang po de lta bu ston pa dang / glu
19a4('bum): dang sil snyan gyis skye bo dga' bar byed cing / sbyin pa yod dasu gtang ba dang / tshul khrims srung ba dang / bzod pa/ sgrub pa dang / brtson 'grus brtsam pa dang / ting nge 'dzin
19a5('bum): gyis rnam par brtse ba dang / shes rab sgom pa dang / rnam ba 'di dag gis skye bo dga' bar byed cing / rgyal rig sa che zhing mtho ba'i rigs ston pa dang / bram ze che zhing mtho
19a6('bum): ba'i rigs ston pa dang / khyim bdag che zhing mtho ba'i rigs ston pa dang / ri rab ston pa dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams ston pa dang / sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams ston pa dang / 'tshe
19a7('bum): ma'i lha rnams ston pa dang / dga' ldan gyi lha rnams ston pa dang / 'phrul dga'i lha rnams ston pa dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams ston pa dang / tshangs ris kyi lha rnams ston pa dang / tshangs
19a8('bum): lha nye phan gyi lha rnams ston pa dang / tshangs pa kun 'khor gyi lha rnams ston pa dang / tshangs chen gyi lha rnams ston pa dang / snang ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / chung snang gi lha rnams ston pa dang / tshad med
19b1('bum): snang ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / kun snang dang ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / dge ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / chung dge'i lha rnams ston pa dang / tshad med dge shi rnams ston pa dang / dge rgyas kyi lha
19b2('bum): rnams ston pa dang / che ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / chung che'i lha rnams ston pa dang / tshad med che ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / 'bras bu che ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / mi che ba'i lha rnams
19b3('bum): ston pa dang / mi gdung ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / shin tu mthong ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / gya nom snang ba'i lha rnams ston pa dang / 'og min gyi lha rnams ston pa dang / nam mkha' mtha'
19b4('bum): yas skye mched kyi lha rnams ston pa dang / rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched kyi lha rnams ston pa dang / cung zad med pa'i skye mched kyi lha rnams ston pa dang / 'du shes med 'du shes
19b5('bum): med min skye mched kyi lha rnams ston pa dang / gzugs med pa rnams ston pa dang / rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu rnam sa ston pa dang / lan cig phyir 'ong ba rnams dang / phyir mi 'o/ 
19b6('bum): ba dang / dgra bcom pa dang / rang sangs rgyas mang po rnams ston cing / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams sems dang po bskyed pa nas nye bar bzung ste/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa
19b7('bum): la spyod pa dang / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa
19b8('bum): la spyod pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa dang / nang stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / phyi stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / phyi nang stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang
20a1('bum): chen po stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / don dam pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / 'dus byas stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / mtha' las 'das pa
20a2('bum): bstong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / rang bzhin stong pa nyid la spyod
20a3('bum): pa dang chos thams cad stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la spong ba dang / dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / ngo bo nyid
20a4('bum): stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la spyod pa dang / dran pa nye bar bzhag pa rnams la/ spyod pa dang / yang dag par spyong pa rnams la spyod pa dang / 
20a5('bum): rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la spyod pa dang / dbang po rnams la spyod pa dang / stobs rnams la spyod pa dang / byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la spyod pa dang / 'phags pa'i lam
20a6('bum): yan lag brgyad pa la spyod pa dang / 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la spyod pa dang / bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug pa rnams la spyod pa dang / sa dang / 
20a7('bum): po yong su rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa gnyis pa yong su rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa gsum pa yongasasu rdzogs pa byed pa dang / sa bzhi pa yongasasu rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa lnga pa yongasu rdzog
20a8('bum): par byed pa dang / sa drug pa yongasu rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa bdun pa yongasasu rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa brgyad pa yongasasu rdzogs par byed pa dang / sa dgu pa yong su rdzogs par byed pa dang / 
20b1('bum): sa bcu pa yongasu rdzogs par byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med par 'jug pa dang / mngon par shes pa rnams mngon par sgrub pa dang / mngon par shes pa de dag gis rnam par 'artse ba dang / 
20b2('bum): 'jig rten gyi khams snang bar byed pa dang / sems can yongasu smin par byed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yong su dag par byed pa dang / yan lag dang nying lag yongasu gtong ba dang / dka'
20b3('bum): ba'i spyod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams yongasu bsgrub pa dang / mi 'jigs pa rnams yongasu sgrub pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa rnams yongasu sgrub pa dang / sangs
20b4('bum): rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams yongasu sgrub pa'o// byams pa chen po mngon par sgrub pa dang / snying rje chen po mngon par bya sgrub pa de dag kyang ston cing sangs rgyas kyi sku yan lag dang
20b5('bum): nyid lag thams cad yongasu rdzogs pa ston pa ni ngo mtshar rje/ 'o zhes ngo mtshar rjer 'dzin to// de la skyes bu mkhas/ shing gsal la yid rdo ba dang ldan pa/ dpyod pa dam pa dang / 
20b6('bum): ldan pa rnams ni 'di lta ste/ 'di la chos gang yang dmigasu med na/ mi 'di de ltar med pa'i chos kyis skye bo mang po 'dir ga dga' bar byed pa ni/ ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos so skye
20b7('bum): ster sems can 'di dag ni dngos po med pa la dngos por 'du shes pa'o// zhes bya bar de dag gis shes pa 'byung ngo // rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po

33b4('bum): bapa yin gzhan yang rtag tu rgyun mi chad par byams pa sgom pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyangartag tu rgyun mi chad par snying rje la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang /

33b6('bum): chad par dga' ba bsgom pa la yang dag par bskul ba yin// bdag kyang rtag tu rgyun mi chad par btang snyoms la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rtag tu rgyun min par btang snyoms la yang dag par
33b7('bum): bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang rtag tu nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched kyi snyoms
33b8('bum): par 'jug pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms par 'jug pa yin/ gzhan yang rnam shes mtha' yas skye
34a1('bum): mched kyi stoms par 'gru pa la yang dag par bskul ba yin// bdag kyang chung bang med pa'i skye mjed kyi snyoms par 'gyu ba la snyoms par 'gru ba yin/ gzhan yang / 
34a2('bum): chung zad med pa'i skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la yang dag par bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms par 'jug pa
34a3('bum): yin/ gzhan yang 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa la yang dag par bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan
34a4('bum): yang sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang tshul khrims kyi pha
34a5('bum): rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par
34a6('bum): bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang bsam
34a7('bum): gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa
34a8('bum): yin gzhan yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la yang dag par bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang nang stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang nang stong pa nyid la yang dag par bskul ba
34b1('bum): yin bdag kyang phyi stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang phyi stong pa nyid la yang dag par bskul ba yin/ bdag kyang phyi nang stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang phyi nang stong pa nyid/ 
34b2('bum): la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang stong pa nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang chen po stong pa nyid
34b3('bum): sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang chen po stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang don dam pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang don dam pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par
34b4('bum): skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'dus byas stong pa nyid sgom pa yin pa/ gzhan yang 'dus byas stong pa nyid la yang dag dpar skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid
34b5('bum): sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang mtha' las
34b6('bum): 'das pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin// 
34b7('bum): bdag kyang dor ba med pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rang bzhin stong
34b8('bum): pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin// bdag kyang chos thams cad stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang chos thams cad stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rang gi mtshan nyid
35a1('bum): stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang
35a2('bum): mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dngos po med pa stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba
35a3('bum): yin/ bdag kyang ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid sgom pa yin/ 
35a4('bum): gzhan yang dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dran pa nye bar / gzhag pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang dran pa nye bar
35a5('bum): gzhag pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang yang dag par spong ba rnams sgom pa yin/ ga zhan yang yang dag par spong ba rnams la yang dag par
35a6('bum): skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dbang po rnams sgom pa yin/ 
35a7('bum): gzhan yang dbang po rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang stobs rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang stobs rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams
35a8('bum): sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang byang chub kyi yan lag rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'phags pa'i lam ya/ 
35b1('bum): lag brgyad pa la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag
35b2('bum): kyang 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams sgom pa yin/ gzhan yang 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rnam par thar pa brgyud la slob pa yin// gzhan
35b3('bum): yang rnam par thar pa brgyad la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par
35b4('bum): 'jug pa lnga yang dag par skul ba yin// bdag kyang mdo na pa shes pa rnams la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang/ dmangon par shes pa rnams la yang dag bAr stsal ba yin/ 
35b5('bum): bdag kyang ting nge 'dzin rnams la slob pa yin gzhanayang ting nge 'dzin rnams la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang gzungs kyi rnams la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang
35b6('bum): gzungs kyi sgo rnams la yang dag par skul pa yin/ bdag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la yang dag par skul yin/ 
35b7('bum): bdag kyang mi 'jigs pa bzhi la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mi 'jigs pa bzhi la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang so so
35b8('bum): yang dag par rig pa bzhi la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang byams pa chen po la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang byams pa chen po la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang snying rje chen po la slob pa yin/ 
36a1('bum): gzhan yang snying rje chen po la yang dag par sprul ba yin// bdag kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang sangs rgyas kyi/ 
36a2('bum): chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang mi chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang mi chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis la yang dag par
36a3('bum): skul ba yin/ bdag kyang dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu la slob pa yin/ gzhan yang dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu la yang dag par skul ba yin/ bdag kyang rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'i shes pa
36a4('bum): spyad cing de la mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang lan cig/ phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i shes bskyed cing / de la yang mi
36a5('bum): gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang phyir mi 'ong / ba'i 'bras bu'i shes pa skyed cing de la yang mi gnas pa yin/ 
36a6('bum): gzhan yang phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu'i shes pa skyed cing de la yang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang dgra bcom pa nyid la 'god/ 
36a7('bum): pa yin/ bdag kyang rang byang chub kyi shes pa skyed cing de la yang mi gnas pa yin/ gzhan yang rang byang chub la 'god pa yin/ bdag kyang bla na med pa yang dag
36a8('bum): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi lam skyed pa yin/ gzhan yang lam de la 'dems shing rjes su ston pa dang / gzhog cing 'dul ba dang 'god pa yin te/ rab 'byor de ltar byang chub
36b1('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ sems dang po skyed pa nas nye bar gzung ste/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid la gnas shing / sems
36b2('bum): can rnams kyi don byed pa'i tshe/ nam yang las med par gnas pa ma yin no// gsol pa bcom ldan 'das gal te de ltar chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis stong pa lags na/ 8
36b3('bum): bzhin stong pa nyid ni sems can yang mi dmigs so// chos kyang mi dmigs// chos ma lags pa yang mi dmigs na/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
36b4('bum): chen po rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi don du yang dag dpar 'jug pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'astsal pa/ rab 'byor de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ ji skad du
36b5('bum): smras pa bzhin no// chos thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis ste pa ste/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid la ni/ sems can mi dmig so// chos mi dmig so// chos ma yin pa mi dmigs
36b6('bum): rab 'byor gal te chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis stong pa zhig ma yin na ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang rang bzhin stong pa nyid la gnas par mi 'gyur te/ bla na med pa yang dag
36b7('bum): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas kyang chos rnams rang bzhin gyis stong par mi ston to// rang bzhin gyis stong pa'i chos de dag kyang gang zhe na/ rab 'byor gzugs ni rang bzhin
36b8('bum): gyis stong ngo // tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du shes ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du byed ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor mig ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
37a1('bum): rna ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna ni rang bzhin gyis snong ngo // lce ni rang bzhin gyis snong ngo // lus ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor gajug
37a2('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sgra ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dri ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ro ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // reg ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chos ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor mig
37a3('bum): gi rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce'i rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
37a4('bum): lus kyi rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor/ dmig gi 'dus te reg gi rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i 'dus
37a5('bum): te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce'i 'dus te reg pa ni rang zhin gyis stong ngo // lus kyi 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyi
37a6('bum): stong ngo / yid kyi 'dus te reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang
37a7('bum): bzhin gyis stong ngo // sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen
37a8('bum): gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor sa'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chu'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis
37b1('bum): stong ngo // me'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rlung gi khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // na mkha'i khams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par shes pa'i khams ni rang bzhin
37b2('bum): gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor ma rig pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'du byed ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par shes pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ming dang gzugs ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
37b3('bum): skye mched drug ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // reg pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshor ba ni rang bzhin stong ngo // sred pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ldan pa ni rang bzhin gyis sbyong ngo // srid pa ni rang bzhi/ 
37b4('bum): gyis stong ngo // skye ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rga shi ni rang de bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin dab ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin
37b5('bum): ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bsam gtan gyis pha
37b6('bum): tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor nang stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // phyi stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // phyi nang stong
37b7('bum): pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chen po stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // don dam pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'dus byas stong pa
37b8('bum): nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis
38a1('bum): stong ngo 'do ba med pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // chos thams cad stong pa nyid ni nga bzhin gyis
38a2('bum): stongango // rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ngo bo nyid
38a3('bum): stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rab 'byor dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 
38a4('bum): yang dag par spong ba rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dadabang po rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // stobs rnams ni
38a5('bum): rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // byang chub kyi yan lag rnams ni rardza bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // 'phags pa'i bden pa
38a6('bum): rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // bsam gtan rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // tshad med pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis
38a7('bum): stong ngo // rnam par thar pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa
38a8('bum): mang ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mngon par shes pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // ting 'dzin rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // gzungs kyi sgo rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa'i stongs
38b1('bum): rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong // mi 'jigs pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // so so yang dag par rig pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong // byams pa chen po na rang bzhin gyis sdong ngo // snyi chen
38b2('bum): nirang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dga' ba chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // btang snyoms chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // mi chen po'i
38b3('bum): mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu
38b4('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni rang de bzhin gyis stong ngo // dgra bcom pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rang byang chub ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // lam gyi
38b5('bum): rnam pa shes pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // rnam pa tham sa cad mkhyen pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // de bas na byang chub sems phes chen po/ shes rab kyi pha
38b6('bum): rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ phung po lnga ni rang bzhin gyis spyong ngo // zhes bya bar chos ston to// skye mched bcu gnyis ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // zhes bya bar chos ston to// khams bco brgyad
38b7('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // zhes bya bar chos ston to// pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong
38b8('bum): ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// stong pa nyid thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// yang dag
39a1('bum): par spong ba bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo // zhes bya bar chos ston to// dbang po lnga ni rang bzhin gyis
39a2('bum): stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// stobs lnga ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// byang chub kyi yan lag bdun ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// 'phags
39a3('bum): pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// bsam gtan bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// tshad med pa bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong
39a4('bum): ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// rnam par thar pa brgyad ni rang bzhin gyis stong / 
39a5('bum): ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// mthar gyis gnas pa'i ste/ mas par 'jug pa dgu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / 
39a6('bum): mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// mngon par shes pa lnga ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// ting nge 'dzin thams cad ni rang bzhin
39a7('bum): gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// gzungs kyi sgo thams cad ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar
39a8('bum): chos ston to// mi 'jigs pa bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// byams pa chen po
39b1('bum): ni rang bzhin gyis stong zhes bya bar chos ston to// snying chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong shes bya bar chos ston to// dga' ba chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ba zhes bya ba chos ston to// bang
39b2('bum): snyoms chen po ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// mi chen po'i mtshan sum cu
39b3('bum): rtsa gnyis ni rang bzhin gyis stong pa zhes bya bar chos ston to// dpe byang bzang po brgyad du ni rang bzhin gyis stong zhes bya bar chos ston to// rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu ni rang bzhin gyis stong panam/ 
39b4('bum): bya bar chos ston to// lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni rang de bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston
39b5('bum): dgra tsam pa nyi na bzhin gyis snang bzhis ba chos ston to//  byang chu ni / lam gyi rnam pa shes pa kyi rang sngon gyis sto
39b6('bum): zhes bya bar chos ston to// rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes bya bar chos ston to// bag chags kyi mtshams sbyor ba thams cad spong ba ni rang bzhin gyis stong ngo zhes

82b1('bum): mi byed do// mi 'jigs pa rnams stong pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi stong pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug
82b2('bum): par mi byed do// byams pa chen po stong pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// snying rje chen po stong pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// 
82b3('bum): sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams stong pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu stong pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam pa/ 
82b4('bum): 'khrug par mi byed do// lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu stong pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug/ dpar mi byed do// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu stong pa 'am
82b5('bum): 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// dgra bcom pa nyid stong pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang byang chub stong/ 
82b6('bum): pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub stong pa 'am/ 'on tam mi stong zhes bya bar rnam par 'khrug
82b7('bum): par mi byed do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni gzugs so// 'di ni gzugs kyi stong pa nyid do// zhes gzugs rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang
82b8('bum): bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni tshor ba'o// 'di ni tshor ba'i stong pa nyid do zhes tshor ba rnams 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni 'du sheso// 'di ni 'du shes
83a1('bum): stong pa nyid do// zhes 'du shes rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni 'du byed do// 'do ni 'du byed kyi stong pa nyid do// zhes 'du byed rnam par lats+tsha/ 
83a2('bum): par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rnam par shes pa'o// 'di ni rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes rnam par shes pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni mi
83a3('bum): go/ 'di ni mig gi stong pa nyid do zhes mig rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni rna ba'o// 'di ni rna ba'i stong pa nyid do// zhes rna ba rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin
83a4('bum): stong pa nyid ni 'di ni sna'o// 'di ni sna'i stong pa nyid do// zhes smra rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni lce'o 'di ni lu'i stong pa nyid do zhes/ lce rnam par
83a5('bum): 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni lus// 'di ni lus kyi stong pa nyid do// zhes lus rnam par 'dru/ ga par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni yid do// 'di ni

83a7('bum): stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni sgra'o// 'di ni sgra'i stong pa nyid do zhes/ sgra rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni dri'o// 'di ni dri'i stong pa nyid do zhes/ dri rnam par 'khrug par mi

84a1('bum): par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ 'di ni sna'i 'dus te reg pa'o// 'di ni sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes sna'i 'dus te reg pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do//

124a2('bum): nyid med do// skye ba mi sbyor mi 'byed do/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i skye ba la ngo bo nyid med do// rga shi mo sbyar mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di lta
124a3('bum): gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rga shi la ngo bo nyid medo// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i sbyin pa'i pha
124a4('bum): rol tu phyin pa la ngo bo nyid med do// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i tshul khrims kyi
124a5('bum): pha rol tu phyin pa la ngo bo nyid med do// bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i bzod pa'i pha rol tu
124a6('bum): phyin pa la ngo bo nyid medo// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ngo bo
124a7('bum): nyid medo// bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bor bya ba'i bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ngo bo nyid med do// shes
124a8('bum): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ngo bo nyid medo// nang stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ 
124b1('bum): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i nang stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// byi stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba
124b2('bum): 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i phyi stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid medado// phyi nang stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i phyi nang stong pa nyid la ngo bo
124b3('bum): nyid med do// stong pa nyid stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i stong pa nyid stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// chen po stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi
124b4('bum): 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i chen po stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid medo// don dam pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 
124b5('bum): de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i don dam pa stongapa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// 'dus byas stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang
124b6('bum): sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i 'dus byas stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye
124b7('bum): bar bya ba'i 'dus mo byas stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya
124b8('bum): ba'i mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bor bya ba'i
125a1('bum): thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// dor ba med pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ da
125a2('bum): bar bya ba'i dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rang bzhin stong/ 
125a3('bum): pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// chos thams cad stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i chos thams cad stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid
125a4('bum): med do// rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am// dbye bar bya ba'i rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid
125a5('bum): med do// mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyor ba'am// dbye bar bya ba'i mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med// 
125a6('bum): dngos po med pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid medo// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi
125a7('bum): 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid med do// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di
125a8('bum): ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang
125b1('bum): sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi la ngo bo nyid med do// yang dag par spong ba bzhi mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i yang dag
125b2('bum): par spong ba bzhi la ngo bo nyid med do// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi mo sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi la ngo bo nyid med
125b3('bum): do/ dbang po lnga mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltor gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i dbang po lnga la ngo bo nyid med do// stobs lnga mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di
125b4('bum): ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i stobs lnga la ngo bo nyid med de// byang chub kyi yan lag bdun mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya
125b5('bum): ba'i byang chub kyi yan lag bdun la ngo bo nyid med do// 'phag sa pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar
125b6('bum): bya ba'i 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la ngo bo nyid med do// 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i 'phags
125b7('bum): ba'i bden pa bzhi la ngo bo nyid med do// bsam gtan bzhi mi spror mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i bsam gtan bzhi la ngo bo nyid med do// / 
125b8('bum): tshad med pa bzhi mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i tshad med pa bzhi la ngo bo nyid med do// gzugs med pa'i snyoms par
126a1('bum): 'jug pa bzhi mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi la jom
126a2('bum): nyid med do// rnam par thar pa brgyad mi sbyor mi 'byed do/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rnam par thar pa brgyad la ngo bo nyid med// 
126a3('bum): do// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gong sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya pa'i mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par
126a4('bum): 'jug pa dgu la ngo bo nyid med do// rnam par thar pa'i sgo ste ba nyid dang / mtshan mo med pa dang / smon pa med pa ma sbyor mo 'byed do/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba
126a5('bum): 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa la ngo bo nyid/ mdo// mngon par shes pa rnams mi sbyor mi 'byed de/  tsa
126a6('bum): phyir zhe na/ doni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dpe bar bya ba'i mngon par shes pa rnams la ngo bo nyid med// ting nge 'dzin rnams mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyor ba'am// 
126a7('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i ting 'dzin rnams la ngo bo nyid med do// gzungs kyi sgo rnams mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i gzungs kyi sgo rnams lango
126a8('bum): nyid med// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu ma sbyar mi 'byed/ daci'i phyir no na// de ni 'di ltar gang sbyor ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams la ngo bo nyid med do// 
126b1('bum): mi 'jigs pa bzhi mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i mi 'jigs pa rnams la ngo bo nyid med do// so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi mi sbyor mi
126b2('bum): 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i so so yang dag par rig pa rnams la ngo bo nyid med do// snying rje chen po mi sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar/ 
126b3('bum): gang sbyar ba 'am/ dpe bar bya ba'i snying rje chen po la ngo bo nyid med do// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad ma sbyor mi 'byed/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar
126b4('bum): bya ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams la ngo bo nyid da med do// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das chos gang la yang gang sbyar ba'am/ dbye bar bgyi ba'i ngo bo nyid ma mchis
126b5('bum): no/ gang la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos/ bslab par bgyis pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ltar mngon par 'grub par 'gyur/ shes rab tu
126b6('bum): rol tu phyin pa la ma bslabs par ni/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mi nu so// bcom ldan/ 
126b7('bum): 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu de de bzhin te/ de de bzhin no// ji skad du smras pa de bzhin te/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ma bslabs par/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
126b8('bum): pos/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mi nus te/ de yang thabs mkhas pas yin gyi/ thabs mi mkhas pas ma yin// sha ra dwa ti'i bu gal te/ 
127a1('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ chos gang la la zhig gi ngo bo nyid dmigs na ni de'i phyir 'dzin par yang
127a2('bum): 'gyur na/ 'on te mi dmigs na/ 'di gzugs so// 'di ni tshor ba'o// 'di ni 'du shes so// 'di ni 'du byed do// 'di ni rnam par shes pa'o zhes bya bar yang ci zhig gzung / 'di dag ni skye mched
127a3('bum): rnam so// 'di dag ni khams rnam so// 'di ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'o// 'di ni ma rig pa'o// 'di ni 'du byed do// 'di ni rnam par shes pa'o// 'di ni mang dang gzug so// 'di ni skye mched
127a4('bum): drug go// 'di ni reg pa'o// 'di ni tshor ba'o// 'di ni sred pa'o// 'di ni len pa'o// 'di ni srid pa'o// 'di ni skye ba'o// / 'di ni rga shi'o// 'di ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di na
127a5('bum): tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phan ba'o// 'di ni bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni
127a6('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni nang stong pa nyid do// 'di ni phyi stong pa nyid do// 'di ni phyi nang stong pa nyid do// 'di ni stong pa nyid stong pa nyid do// 'di ni chen po stong pa nyid do// 'di dag ni don dam
127a7('bum): pastong pa nyid do// 'di ni 'dus byas stong pa nyid do// 'di ni 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid do// 'di ni mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni dor ba med
127a8('bum): pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni rang bzhin stong pa nyid// 'di na chos thams cad stong pa nyid// 'di ni rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid do// 'don mo dmigs pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni dngos po med pa stong pa nyid
127b1('bum): do// 'di ni nga ba nyid stong pa nyid do// 'di ni dngos po med pa'i ngo ba nyid stong pa nyid do// 'di dag na dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi'o// 'di dag ni yang dag par spong ba shi'o// 'di dag ni rdzu 'phrul
127b2('bum): rkang pa bzhi'o// 'di dag na dbang po lnga'o// 'di dag ni stobs lnga'o// 'di dag ni byang chub kyi yan lag bdun no// 'di dag ni 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'o// 'di dag ni 'phags pa'i
127b3('bum): bden pa bzhi'o// 'di dag ni byams pa chen po'o// 'di dag ni bsam gtan bzhi'o// 'di dag ni tshad med pa bzhi'o// 'di dag ni gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi'o// 'di dag
127b4('bum): ni rnam par thar pa brgya do// 'di dag ni mthar gyis gnas dpa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu'o// 'di dag ni rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon
127b5('bum): pa med pa'o// 'di ni mngon par shes pa rnamaso// 'di dag ni ting 'dzin rnamaso// 'di dag ni gzungs kyi sgo rnam so// 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu
127b6('bum): 'di dag ni mi 'jigs pa'o// 'di dag ni so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi'o// 'di dag ni snying rje chen po'o// 'di dag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad do// 'di dag ni rgyun tu zhugs
127b7('bum): pa'i 'bras bu'o// 'di dag ni lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// 'di ni phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// 'di ni dgra bcom pa nyid// 'di ni rang byang chub bo// 'di ni lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid do// 
127b8('bum): 'di ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid do zhes bya bar yang ci zhig gzung ste/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni gzung du med pa'o// bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni gzung du med
128a1('bum): pa'o// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni gzung du med pa'o// bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni bzung du med pa'o// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni gzung du med
128a2('bum): pa'o// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni gzung du med pa'o// nang stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// phyi stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// phyi nang stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// stong pa nyid
128a3('bum): stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// chen po stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// don dam pa stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// 'dus byas stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// 'dus ma byas
128a4('bum): stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// dor ba med pa
128a5('bum): stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni/ gzung du med pa'o// chos thams cad stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid ni gzung
128a6('bum): du med pa'o// mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// dngos po med pa stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid
128a7('bum): ni gzung du med pa'o// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi ni gzung du med pa'o// yang dag par spong ba bzhi ni gzung du med pa'o// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi ni gzung du med pa'o// dbang po lnga ni gzung
128a8('bum): du med pa'o// stobs lnga ni gzung du med pa'o// byang chub kyi yan lag bdun ni gzung du med pa'o// 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ni gzung du med pa'o// 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi ni
128b1('bum): gzung du med pa'o// bsam gtan bzhin gzung du med pa'o// tshad med pa bzhini gzung du med pa'o// gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhin gzung du med pa'o// rnam par thar pa ba/ 
128b2('bum): ni gzung du med pa'o// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu ni gzung du med pa'o// rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa ni gzung du med
128b3('bum): pa'o// mngon par shes pa rnams ni gzung du med pa'o// ting 'dzin rnams ni gzung du med pa'o// gzung kyi sgo rnams ni gzung du med pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu ni gzung du med// 
128b4('bum): pa'o// mi 'jigs pa bzhi ni gzung du med pa'o// so so yang / dag par rig pa bzhi ni gzung du med pa'o// byams pa chen po ni gzung du med pa'o// snying rje chen po ni gzung du med
128b5('bum): pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad ni gzung du med pa'o// sha ra dwa ti'i bu de ni gzung du med pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ste/ 'di ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// de la
128b6('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos/ bslabs par bya ste/ de la slob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos bslab pa yang mi dmigs na/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu
128b7('bum): phyin pa lta ci smos/ byang chub kyi chos rnams lta yang ci smos/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams lta yang ci smos/ rang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams lta yang ci smos/ nyan thos kyi chos rnams lta yang ci/ 
128b8('bum): smos/ so so skye bo'i chos rnams lta yang ci smos/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu de ni 'di ltar chos gang la yang ngo bo nyid medado// de ltar chos thams cad dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid la so so
129a1('bum): skye bo'i chos ni gang / rgyun tu zhugs pa ni gang zhig yod/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba ni gang zhig yod/ phyir mi 'ong ba ni gang zhig yod/ dgra bcom pa ni gang zhig yod
129a2('bum): rang sangs rgyas ni gang zhig yod/ byang chub sems dpa' ni gang zhig yod/ de bzhin gsheg pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ni gang zhig yod/ gal te gang zag de
129a3('bum): dag dmigs su med na/ chos gang gis so so skye bo 'am/ rgyun tu zhugs pa 'am/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba 'am/ phyir mi 'ong ba'am/ dgra bcom pa'am/ rang sangs rgyas sam/ byang chub
129a4('bum): sems dpa' 'am/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas zhes bya bar brjod pa'i chos de dag 'byung bar yang ga la 'gyur// 
129a5('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa/ bam po nya/ sa brgya gyi dgu pa/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad dngos po ma mchis pa la/ 'di ni so so'i skye bo
129a6('bum): zhes bgyi ba nas/ 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyaso zhes bgyi ba'i bar du 'byung ba ci'i slad dmigs par 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
129a7('bum): stsal pa/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu ci gzugs kyi dngos po gang la byis pa so so skye bo rnams mngon par zhen par 'gyur ba de lta bu yod dam/ yod par gyur tam/ yod par 'gyur ram/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan
129a8('bum): 'das phyin ci log me btogs par de ni ma lag so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu ci tshor ba'i dngos po gang la byis pa so so skye bo rnams mngon par zhen par gyur
129b1('bum): pade lta bu yod dam/ yod par gyur ram/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das phyin ci log ma btogs par/ de ni ma lag so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sha ra dadwa ti'i bu ci 'du shes kyi dngos
129b2('bum): po gang la/ byis pa so so skye bo rnams mngon par zhen par gyur pa de lta bu yod dam/ yod par gyur tam/ yod par 'gyur ram/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das phyin ci log ma gtogs par de ni ma
